 The Union Minister said that a total of 123 ghats, 65 crematoriums, 8 water infrastructure and 35 other projects have been started
 uma bharti ne kaha ki namaami gange kaarykram 20,000 karod rupee kii laagat se shuru kiya gaya he jisamen nae prayaason ke liye 12,728 karod rupee shaamil hai
 351 specifically under this
 42 karod rupee kii sweekrut laagat vaali 12 pariyojnaayen manjuur kii gai hai

 The minister said that during the sixth meeting of the National Ganga River Basin Authority on 4 July 2016, all the members including representatives of the five member states were present in which they agreed to prepare the Ganga Act with the consent of the states
 uma ne kaha ki jab vah mantri nahin thi tab unhone sabhi saansadon ko ganga jal bheja tha or ganga ke vishay par sahyog maanga tha
 It was then unanimously supported by everyone
 ab jab sansad main kanoon banane ke liye vidheyak lekar aaengi tab usee tarah se sarvasammati se use paarit karne kii sabhi se prarthana karengi
 In response to a question, he said that the worship material put in the river is not the main factor of pollution of the Ganges river
 yah pujan saamagree nadi pravaah ke saath swayan bah jaati he
 But when the flow of the river is reduced or interrupted due to other pollution, this worship material gets collected at one place and increases pollution
 unhone kaha ki ganga nadi ke pradooshan kaa mukhya kaaran iske kinare basii audyogic ikaayiyon dwaara isamen daalaa jane vaala pradooshit jal evam kachra tathaa sivej he
 After the present government came to power, in September, after meeting with these polluting units, they were instructed to take measures to prevent pollution in the Ganges
 uma ne kaha ki sarkaar ganga nadi main pradooshan ko rokane ke liye ek kanoon laane par vichaar kar rahi he jisamen pradooshan failaane vaali ikaayiyon ke khilaaf kade praavdhaan honge
 Uma Bharti said that a survey conducted by the Central Pollution Control Board and the State Pollution Control Board revealed 764 completely polluting industries generating 501 MLD waste water in the Ganges basin
 kendriya pradooshan niyantran board ne pradooshan failaane vaale udyogon ko notice jari kiye hai
 He said that the Narendra Modi government is committed to making Ganga pollution free
 unhone kaha ki sarkaar ke is sankalp ko desh evam videshon main kaaphi samarthan mil rahaa he
 Uma said that the Central Pollution Control Board has been given Rs 196 crore to install the equipment for the purpose of checking the Ganges water quality at various places

 He said that the main reason for the pollution of the river Ganga is the polluted water and waste and sewage dumped by industrial units located on its banks

 Uma said that the government is considering a law to curb pollution in the Ganges river which would have stricter provisions against the polluting units
 uma bharti ne kaha ki kendriya pradooshan niyantran board evam rajya pradooshan niyantran board dwaara kiye gayi surveykshan main ganga basin main 501 emeldi apshisht jal utpann karne vaale 764 puri tarah pradooshnakaari udyogon kaa pataa chalaa he
 The Central Pollution Control Board has issued notices to polluting industries
 unhone kaha ki narendra modi sarkaar ganga ko pradooshan mukt karne ke liye patibaddh he

 so, desh main falte-phoolate or mahilaon ko bahut badi sankhya main rojgaar dene vaale - lagbhag 3 karod 10 lakh mahilaon ko, jo uski kul kaaryashakti kaa 70 fisadi hissaa hai - garment udyog kaa yah ek andhera pahalu he
 
 
 Government also has special attention towards this industry
 
 
 pichley hi maheene centre sarkaar ne 6,000 karod rupee kaa package die jane kii bhi ghoshnaa kii thi, or ab smriti irani kii kapadaa mantri ke rup main niyukti bhi saaf karti he ki bharat kii aarthik vruddhi main kapadaa udyog ke yogadan par vishesh dhyaan diya ja rahaa he
 
 
 But the kind of incidents that came to our knowledge gives a clear indication that even though the number of women working in this industry is high, they work in an environment where they are constantly forced to have sex
 goes
 
 
 unhen yon pratadna, or yahaan tak ki balaatkaar kaa bhi saamana karnaa padataa he, taaki ve naukari paa saken, yaa apni naukari bachaae rakh saken
 
 
 
 
 
 or navita, ratna or sushmanta hi chand ve naam nahin hai, jinhone iskaa saamana kiya
 
 
 We talked to dozens of women in the Karnataka and Gurgaon centers that exported nearly one-third of this industry
 
 
 lagbhag sabhi ne milte-julate anubhav bayaan kiye
 
 
 Some came in front of the camera, but some are so scared that they do not want to make the matter public
 
 
 euke sthit enjio 'sisters of chenj' dwaara karnataka ke garment udyog ko lekar sthaneey saajheedaar 'munnade' (munnade) ke saath milakar kiye ek adhyayan main paaya gaya ki har 14 main se ek mahila garment udyog karmi ko shaareerik hinsa kaa shikaar hona padaa he
 
 
 According to the study published last month, one out of every seven female workers has been victimized or raped, or forced to have sex
 
 
 yahaan lagata he ki yon hinsa ke khilaaf bane nae kanoon, jinke tahat kaam karne kii har jagah par andruni shikaayat cameti honi hi chahie, sirf kaagaz par hi rah gaye hai
 
 
 Shanti, who works for the 'empress', told us, "the Empress Company has such a committee for women, but that is for the nominal
 
 
 cameti main bhi mahilaon ko itnaa zyaada torchar kiya gaya, ki ve kaam chhodkar jane ke liye majaboor ho gayi
 
 
 " kisi bhi brands yaa export company ne hamaare sawaalon kaa jawaab khabar likhe jane tak nahin diya he
 
 
 But Gautam Nair, head of one of Gurgaon's garment associations, says, "the international brands we work with audit our work and environment
 
 
 or ye antarrashtriya brands kaam ke anukool maahaul ko lekar kaaphi samvedansheel hote hai
 
 
 The rules of work should also be according to the existing laws, some of which are even stricter than the Indian laws
 
 
 or kaam kii jagah par yon utpeedan hamaare dwaara kiye jane vaale audit kaa behad mahatvapurn pahalu hota he
 
 
 " bahut-si mahilaon ne hamen bataaya ki jis vakt ye brands audit karne ke liye aate hai, mahilaon ko sikhaaya jaataa he ki kaise unhen auditoron ke saamne saaf-suthere maahaul kaa bhram paidaa karnaa he
 
 
 The comments jinhone bhi himmat jutakar awaz uthaai, unhen budtameezi or beizzati kaa saamana karnaa pad saktaa he, yaa mumkin he, unki naukari hi achaanak khatm kar di jaae
 
 
 While trying to stop her tears in Bengaluru, garment industry worker Manjula told us how she had become a part of a local union, and because of that she was harassed by her bosses over and over, and eventually she quit work
 She was forced
 
 
 duusari mahila gita ne bataaya, uski company main uske suparviser ne use 'veshya' kahkar pukaara, kyonki maine uski mere kareeb aane kii koshishon ko thukraa diya
 
 
 She told that he constantly keeps bothering her by asking, 'when her husband is old, why doesn't she leave him
 
 
 ' On the other hand, similar stories are heard in Bangalore, another major center of the garment industry, thousands of miles south of here
 
 
 texport criations main kaam karne vaali ratna ne bataaya ki kaise uske suparviser us din uski peeth zarur 'thapthapate' hai, jis din vah lo-cat blouse pahenti he
 
 
 We also became aware of the fatal form of this torture
 
 
 devaki disains ke liye kaam karne vaali ek yuvati sushmanta ne kathith rup se isliye aatmahatya kar lee thi, kyonki vah apane ek suparviser dwaara lagaataar pareshaan kiye jane se duhkhi ho gai thi
 
 
 So, this is a dark aspect of the garment industry, which thrives in the country and employs vast numbers of women - about 30 million women, who form 70 per cent of its total workforce
 
 
 is udyog kii ore sarkaar kaa bhi khaas dhyaan he
 
 
 Last month, the central government also announced a package of Rs 6,000 crore, and now the appointment of Smriti Irani as textile minister also makes it clear that special attention is being paid to the contribution of textile industry in India's economic growth
 is
 
 
 lekin jis tarah kii ghatnaayen hamaari jaankaree main ain, unase saaf sanket milte hai ki is udyog main kaam karne vaali mahilaon kii sankhya bhale hi zyaada he, lekin ve ek aise maahaul main kaam karti hai, jahaan unhen yon sambandh banane ke liye lagaataar majaboor kiya jaataa he
 
 
 They have to face sexual harassment, and even rape, so that they can get jobs, or retain their jobs
 
 
 
 
 
 And Navita, Ratna and Sushmanta are not the only few who have faced it
 
 
 is udyog kaa lagbhag ek-tihaai hissaa niryaat karne vaale karnataka or gudgaanv centaron main hamane darjanon mahilaon se baat kii
 
 
 Almost everyone reported similar experiences
 
 
 kuch ne camere ke saamne aakar, lekin kuch itani dari hui hai ki baat ko saarvajanik tak nahin karnaa chaahatin
 
 
 a study conducted by uk-based NGO 'sisters of Change' in association with local partner 'munnade' on Karnataka's garment industry found that one in every 14 women garment industry workers has suffered physical violence
 
 
 
 pichley maheene prakashit adhyayan ke mutabik, har saat main se ek mahila karmi ko yaa balaatkaar kaa shikaar hona padaa he, yaa unhen yon sambandh banane ke liye majaboor kiya gaya he
 
 
 It seems that the new laws against sexual violence, under which there should be an internal complaint committee at every place of work, are left only on paper
 
 
 'maharani' ke liye kaam karne vaali shanti ne hamen bataaya, "maharani company main mahilaon ke liye aisi cameti he, lekin vah nammaatr ke liye he
 
 
 Women were also tortured so much in the committee that they were forced to leave work
 
 
 " No brand or export company has answered our questions till the time of writing the news
 
 
 lekin gudgaanv kii garment associationon main se ek ke pramukh gautam nair kehete hai, "ham jin antarrashtriya brandon ke saath kaam karte hai, ve hamaare kaam or maahaul kaa audit karti hai
 
 
 And these international brands are very sensitive to the work environment
 
 
 kaam ke niyam bhi maujuuda kanoonon ke hisaab se hone chahie, jinamein se kuch to bhartiya kanoonon se bhi sakht hai
 
 
 And sexual harassment at the workplace is a very important aspect of our audit
 
 
 " Many women told us that when these brands come to audit, women are taught how to create an illusion of a clean environment in front of auditors
 
 
 tippaniyan Those who muster up the courage may face insults and dishonor, or may be forced to abruptly end their jobs
 
 
 bengaluru main apane aansuon ko rokane kii koshish karte hue garment udyog karmi manjula ne hamen bataaya ki kaise vah ek sthaneey union kaa hissaa ban gai thi, or usee kii vajah se uske maalikon ne baar-baar pareshaan kiya, or aakhirkaar vah kaam chhodane ke liye majaboor ho gai
 
 
 On the other hand, similar stories are heard in Bangalore, another major center of the garment industry, thousands of miles south of here
 
 
 texport criations main kaam karne vaali ratna ne bataaya ki kaise uske suparviser us din uski peeth zarur 'thapthapate' hai, jis din vah lo-cat blouse pahenti he
